<p>by <a href="http://adndevblog.typepad.com/autocad/fenton-webb.html">Fenton Webb</a></p>
<h2 style="margin: 10pt 0in 0pt;"><span style="font-size: x-small;">Here’s a draft White Paper for the Autodesk Autoloader, please feel free to comment but before you do please consider these points:</span></h2>
<p>1) The Autoloader is designed to simplify 90% of all Autodesk application deployments and is built on-top-of any existing plugin architectures. If the Autoloader doesn’t do what you need, feel free to use the old style of deployment. With that said, if the Autoloader doesn’t do what you want, please let ADN know so that the Autoloader team can consider your Use case.</p>
<p>2) The Autoloader is still being enhanced, although the AutoCAD implementation is currently nearing completion. &#0160;The AutoCAD team implemented the first version of the Autoloader with the view of it being adopted by the other Autodesk Product teams – Revit, Inventor, Alias, Vault, 3DS Max, Maya, now all implement the Autoloader plugin architecture.</p>
<p style="margin: 10pt 0in 0pt;">3) Check out this <a href="http://adndevblog.typepad.com/autocad/Downloads/CP2080_PAL.pdf"><span style="color: #0066cc;">PPT</span></a>, it was presented at Autodesk Universityin 2010, it details an AutoCAD specific overview of why we invented the Autoloader.</p>
<h2 style="margin: 10pt 0in 0pt;"><a name="_Toc325119024"></a><span style="line-height: 13pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt;"><span style="color: #4f81bd; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-weight: bold;"><span style="text-decoration: none;">Autodesk Autoloader Overview</span></span></span></span></h2>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><br />The “Autoloader” module is intended to be a universal plugin loading mechanism for all Autodesk products. Exactly how the “Autoloader” works for an individual product may vary depending on the Autodesk product’s needs, however, the basic design and implementation will be the same.</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;">&#0160;</p>
<p><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><a href="http://adndevblog.typepad.com/.a/6a0167607c2431970b017d3f6b8d3e970c-pi"><img alt="image" border="0" height="252" src="/assets/image_642079.jpg" style="background-image: none; padding-top: 0px; padding-left: 0px; display: inline; padding-right: 0px; border-width: 0px;" title="image" width="456" /></a></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-language: zh-cn; mso-no-proof: yes;">&#0160;</span><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">&#0160;</span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">The “Autoloader” plugin mechanism simplifies deployment of your plugin applications. This is done by allowing you to deploy your plugins as a simple package format (a folder structure with a .bundle extension) along with an XML file placed in the root of the folder structure. The XML file contains metadata which describes the components of your plugin inside the folder structure, and how they should be loaded. The metadata XML also contains information about which Autodesk products it runs with, Operating Systems it supports (Mac, Win32, Win64, Web and/or Mobile) and also Autodesk version/series and/or verticals that it runs with. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">The AutoCAD implementation of the “Autoloader” not only supports the loading of plugin runtime modules such as ARX, DBX, LSP, FAS, VLX etc but it also supports the loading of other AutoCAD modules types such as Partial CUIX files, ToolPalettes and more.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Other Autodesk Products utilize the same metadata XML, loaded from the same locations as AutoCAD apps, to describe how to load their own module types. This allows single Apps to define multiple cross product plugins.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">The package (or rather bundle folder structure) is “installed” simply by placing a copy of the bundle in one of the static Autodesk Application Plugin folders on your hard drive, depending on your machine installation requirement, user and/or administrative requirements. The design requires that no registration is done by an installer at all - all App registration is automatically carried out by the host Autodesk Product “Autoloader” component and/or by the loading modules themselves. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">By moving the registration away from the App’s installer to the host product’s “Autoloader”:</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo5;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: arial;"><span style="mso-list: ignore;">1)<span style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 7pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span></span><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Autodesk App installers become much easier to create</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo5;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: arial;"><span style="mso-list: ignore;">2)<span style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 7pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span></span><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Each individual Autodesk product App deployment requirements become uniform, standardized and work the same even on a Mac machine (cross platform)</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo5;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: arial;"><span style="mso-list: ignore;">3)<span style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 7pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span></span><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Individual Autodesk product App registration complexity is removed.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">The folder locations are:</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l5 level1 lfo2;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: symbol;"><span style="mso-list: ignore;"><span style="font-family: Symbol;">·</span><span style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 7pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span></span><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">%APPDATA%/Autodesk/ApplicationPlugins</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 1in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l5 level2 lfo2; mso-add-space: auto;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;;"><span style="mso-list: ignore;"><span style="font-family: Courier New;">o</span><span style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 7pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span></span><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Requires lowest User administrative rights.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 1in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l5 level2 lfo2; mso-add-space: auto;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;;"><span style="mso-list: ignore;"><span style="font-family: Courier New;">o</span><span style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 7pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span></span><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Will not install for all users, only for the current user.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l5 level1 lfo2;"><span lang="FR" style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: symbol; mso-ansi-language: fr;"><span style="mso-list: ignore;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="font-family: Symbol;">·</span><span style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 7pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span></span></span><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ansi-language: fr;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"><span style="color: #000000;">&#0160;</span></span><span lang="FR"><span style="color: #000000;">%ProgramFiles%/Autodesk/ApplicationPlugins (AutoCAD 2012/deprecated in 2013) <br /><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&#0160;</span>%ProgramData%/Autodesk/ApplicationPlugins (AutoCAD 2013)</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 1in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l5 level2 lfo2; mso-add-space: auto;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;;"><span style="mso-list: ignore;"><span style="font-family: Courier New;">o</span><span style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 7pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span></span><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Requires administrative rights to install to as per Windows Vista/7 requirements.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 1in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l5 level2 lfo2; mso-add-space: auto;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;;"><span style="mso-list: ignore;"><span style="font-family: Courier New;">o</span><span style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 7pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span></span><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">However, the need for a secondary installer is removed because the path is not user specific.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">NOTE:</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> To test where %APPDATA% or %ProgramFiles% or %ProgramData% resides on your machine, simply enter the string %APPDATA% or %ProgramFiles% or %ProgramData% into your Windows Explorer address bar.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">The folders previously listed are static, in other words, they are not configurable and cannot be changed. This design ensures that deployment using installer technologies such as Microsoft’s MSI or Apple’s PKG is extremely simple (uses a very simple “CopyTo” protocol), and it also ensures similar deployment methods on other platforms making it fully cross platform. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Also, plugin management tools such as the Autodesk AppManager can very easily control all Autodesk Apps installed on the system because the runtime file reside in the same place. In addition to that, Product Support is also made easier for the same reason.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">NOTE:</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> You may manually copy the package .bundle to one of the folders if required, it’s not necessary to create an installer. However, a professional deployment should have an installer built so that version upgrades and repairs can be done in an easy way.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">NOTE:</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> A single package .bundle can be deployed on multiple operating systems if required. Win32 and Win64 are required as minimum OS support for a bundle. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">All Autodesk “Autoloader” implementations check the static folders in the order they were previously listed, top to bottom, in two specific contexts</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l2 level1 lfo3;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: symbol;"><span style="mso-list: ignore;"><span style="font-family: Symbol;">·</span><span style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 7pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span></span><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Autodesk Product Startup</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l2 level1 lfo3;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: symbol;"><span style="mso-list: ignore;"><span style="font-family: Symbol;">·</span><span style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 7pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span></span><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">While the Autodesk Product is running, and an Application ‘Appears’ in either of the two folders.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 1in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l2 level2 lfo3; mso-add-space: auto;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: &#39;Courier New&#39;;"><span style="mso-list: ignore;"><span style="font-family: Courier New;">o</span><span style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 7pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span></span><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">NOTE:</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> When the running Autodesk Product detects a new application in either of the two static folders, it waits six seconds for any file copying to finish before processing the package. If the installation of the application program files takes more than six seconds it is recommended that you advise your users to close the Autodesk Product before installing.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">When the Autodesk Product finds an application package bundle that hasn’t been processed yet, it opens the XML metadata file describing the App and automatically registers and/or (if required) loads, all of the compatible modules contained within. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">For Autodesk Exchange downloads, deployment of the package is done via a simple MSI installer. For early applications, we ask that you provide Autodesk with the package contents and XML metadata file, and we will build an MSI installer for you using the Autodesk AppPacker tool (currently internal only).</span><a name="_Toc325119025"></a></span></p>
<h2 style="margin: 10pt 0in 0pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _toc325119025;"><span style="line-height: 13pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt;"><span style="color: #4f81bd; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-weight: bold;">Package format and contents</span></span></span></span></h2>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">There is a lot of detail in this document intended to cover some of the more complex applications you might deploy, but the package can be very simple for a basic plugin application. The package format does have a set layout which is interpreted by the product Autoloader, however, there is currently no set schema therefore you can add your own App specific XML settings data to the package meta data, if required.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Here is an example of one of the simplest package formats and accompanying XML metadata file (blue text indicates a folder, black text is a file, explanations in italic):</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.25in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #0070c0;">ExamplePlugin1.bundle </span></span><em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">– The folder containing your plugin will have an extension of .bundle</span></span></em></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 1in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo6; mso-add-space: auto;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: symbol;"><span style="mso-list: ignore;"><span style="font-family: Symbol;">·</span><span style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 7pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span></span><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">PackageContents.xml – <em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">The XML metadata file used to describe the files in the bundle</em></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 1in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo6; mso-add-space: auto;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: symbol;"><span style="mso-list: ignore;"><span style="font-family: Symbol;">·</span><span style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 7pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span></span><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Minimal.lsp – <em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">An AutoCAD AutoLISP file</em></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 1in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo6; mso-add-space: auto;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: symbol;"><span style="mso-list: ignore;"><span style="font-family: Symbol;">·</span><span style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 7pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span></span><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Minimal.cuix – <em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">An AutoCAD CUIX file</em></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 1in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo6; mso-add-space: auto;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: symbol;"><span style="mso-list: ignore;"><span style="font-family: Symbol;">·</span><span style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 7pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span></span><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">FentiCAD.ico – A<em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">n icon used by the Apps store (the file type used can also be .bmp)</em></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 1in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l4 level1 lfo6; mso-add-space: auto;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: symbol; mso-bidi-font-family: symbol;"><span style="mso-list: ignore;"><span style="font-family: Symbol;">·</span><span style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 7pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span></span><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Help.html <em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">– Either the main help file itself or a document referring the user to more detailed help (e.g. online help at your company’s website)</em></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">A simple XML metadata (the PackageContents.xml file) describing an AutoLISP Application which loads on Startup and for each document opened in the session (PerDocument=True).</span></span></p>
<p style="background: white; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 8.0pt;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&lt;?</span></span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 8.0pt;"><span style="color: #a31515;">xml</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 8.0pt;"><span style="color: #ff0000;">version</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 8.0pt;"><span style="color: #0000ff;">=</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 8.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 8.0pt;"><span style="color: #0000ff;">1.0</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 8.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 8.0pt;"><span style="color: #ff0000;">encoding</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 8.0pt;"><span style="color: #0000ff;">=</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 8.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 8.0pt;"><span style="color: #0000ff;">utf-8</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 8.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span></span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 8.0pt;"><span style="color: #0000ff; font-size: 6pt;">?&gt;</span></span></p>

<p style="background: white; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 8.0pt;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&lt;/</span></span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 8.0pt;"><span style="color: #a31515;">ApplicationPackage</span></span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 8.0pt;"><span style="color: #0000ff; font-size: 6pt;">&gt;</span></span></p>
<p style="background: white; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 8.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 6pt;">&#0160;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Note: Notice that all path specifiers are “/” not “\”, and paths are relative to the root .bundle folder. The bundle *must* be self contained where at all possible – none self contained bundles break cross platform compatibility.</span></span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">The package format is simply a folder structure with the root folder having the .bundle extension. You can create whatever subfolder structure you like but we recommend the following folder structure where possible so that the tools the AppStore team uses to build your app installer can follow a standard style. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">The XML metadata file must be called <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">PackageContents.xml</strong> and must also reside in the root folder. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Below is an example plugin folder structure where the App has no OS dependant modules and is also very small (folders are in blue and files are in black)</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.25in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #0070c0;">ExamplePlugin2.bundle</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">PackageContents.xml</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #0070c0;">Contents</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">mainCommands.lsp</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">test.lsp</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #0070c0;">Resources</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 99pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">MypartialCUI.cuix</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 99pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Icon1.ico</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #0070c0;">Help</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 99pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">HelpHome.htm</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 99pt; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&#0160;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">As an example, you can use whatever structure you like, even just placing all files in the root folder. The above could also have been packaged like this:</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.25in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #0070c0;">ExamplePlugin2.bundle</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span lang="FR" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ansi-language: fr;"><span style="color: #000000;">PackageContents.xml</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span lang="FR" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ansi-language: fr;"><span style="color: #000000;">mainCommands.lsp</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span lang="FR" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ansi-language: fr;"><span style="color: #000000;">test.lsp</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span lang="FR" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ansi-language: fr;"><span style="color: #000000;">MypartialCUI.cuix</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span lang="FR" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ansi-language: fr;"><span style="color: #000000;">Icon1.ico</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span lang="FR" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ansi-language: fr;"><span style="color: #000000;">HelpHome.htm</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span lang="FR" style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ansi-language: fr;"><span style="color: #000000;">&#0160;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">NOTE: </span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">However, combining all files into one folder can make it harder to tell what is in the folder and for larger applications it can also lead to load time performance issues, so it is not recommended.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">For ObjectARX applications, where the specific runtime is important, we suggest that you use OS specific folders such as Mac (for Apple Mac), Win32 (for Windows 32-bit) and Win64 (for Windows 64-bit), like this:</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.25in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #0070c0;">ExamplePlugin3.bundle</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">PackageContents.xml</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #0070c0;">Contents</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #0070c0;">Win32 </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">MyArx_win32.arx</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: accent1;"><span style="color: #4f81bd;">Win64</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">MyArx_x64.arx</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: accent1;"><span style="color: #4f81bd;">Mac</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">MyArx.bundle</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: accent1;"><span style="color: #4f81bd;">CrossPlatform</span></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #0070c0;">Help</span></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">If you have multi-version support, then you should include that in version specific folders </span></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-themecolor: accent1;"><span style="color: #4f81bd;">CrossPlatform</span></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: 0.5in;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">test.lsp</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #0070c0;">Resources</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 99pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">MypartialCUI.cuix</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 99pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Icon1.ico</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #0070c0;">Help</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 99pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">HelpHome.htm</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">If you have multi-version, multi-product support in the same bundle, then you should structure your bundle folders like this…</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.25in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #0070c0;">ExamplePlugin3.bundle</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">PackageContents.xml</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #0070c0;">Contents</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #0070c0;">Win32 </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: 0.5in;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #0070c0;">AutoCAD</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #0070c0;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 2;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>2013</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 2in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: 0.5in;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">MyArx_win32.arx</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1.5in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: 0.5in;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"><span style="color: #000000;">&#0160;</span></span><span><span style="color: #0070c0;">2014</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 2in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: 0.5in;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">MyArx_win32.arx</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: 0.5in;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #0070c0;">Revit</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #0070c0;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 2;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>2013</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 2in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: 0.5in;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">MyRevit.addin</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1.5in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: 0.5in;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"><span style="color: #000000;">&#0160;</span></span><span><span style="color: #0070c0;">2014</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 2in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: 0.5in;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">MyRevit.addin</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 2in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: 0.5in;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Etc…</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Additional package examples accompany the example packages later in this document. Once you have completed creating your own .bundle folder structure containing your application and a PackageContents.xml (in the root of the .bundle folder) please send it to us to be put into our standard installation MSI.</span></span></p>
<h2 style="margin: 10pt 0in 0pt;"><a name="_Toc325119026"></a><span style="line-height: 13pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt;"><span style="color: #4f81bd; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-weight: bold;"><span style="text-decoration: none;">PackageContents.xml format</span></span></span></span></h2>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">The PackageContents.xml file contains some basic information about you (the plugin developer) and the application, and specific information about your plugin components – such as load behaviour (load on startup, command invocation, etc), operating systems, and the AutoCAD and vertical releases it is compatible with.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">The following is an example of including basic information in the XML metadata file, followed by a description of the XML elements. You can see more examples in the AutoCAD Customization Guide.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217;"><span style="line-height: 7pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 6pt;">&lt;?xml version=&quot;1.0&quot; encoding=&quot;utf-8&quot;?&gt;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: 13pt; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217;"><span style="line-height: 7pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 6pt;">&lt;ApplicationPackage SchemaVersion=&quot;1.0&quot; ProductType=&quot;Application&quot; </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: 13pt; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217;"><span style="line-height: 7pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;">Name=&quot;SampPackage&quot; </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: 13pt; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217;"><span style="line-height: 7pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;">AppVersion=&quot;1.0.0&quot; </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: 13pt; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217;"><span style="line-height: 7pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;">Description=&quot;Sample packageXml&quot; </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: 13pt; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217;"><span style="line-height: 7pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;">Author=&quot;Fenton Webb&quot; </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: 13pt; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217;"><span style="line-height: 7pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;">Icon=&quot;./Contents/Resources/ProductIcon.ico&quot; </span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: 13pt; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217;"><span style="line-height: 7pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;">HelpFile=&quot;./Contents/Resources/HelpFile.htm&quot; </span></span></span></p>
