<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: 13pt; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217;"><span style="line-height: 7pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&lt;/ComponentEntry&gt;</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: 13pt; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217;"><span style="line-height: 7pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&lt;ComponentEntry AppName=&quot;MyLispApp&quot; ModuleName=&quot;./Contents/Resources/test.lsp&quot; AppDescription=&quot;A very simple lisp file&quot; PerDocument=&quot;False&quot; /&gt;</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: 13pt; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217;"><span style="line-height: 7pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&lt;ComponentEntry ModuleName=&quot;./Contents/Resources/MacCUI.cuix&quot; AppDescription=&quot;Mac Specific CUI File&quot; /&gt;</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: 13pt; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217;"><span style="line-height: 7pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&#0160; </span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&lt;/Components&gt;</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: 13pt; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217;"><span style="line-height: 7pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 6pt;">&#0160;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217;"><span style="line-height: 7pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 6pt;">&lt;/ApplicationPackage&gt;</span></span><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">&#0160;</strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Definitions of element:</span></span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt;">NOTE:</span></span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 10.5pt;"> XML attributes are case sensitive</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Element name:</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> ApplicationPackage (required)</span></span></p>
<p><span style="font-family: times new roman,times; font-size: 10pt;">You can specify RuntimeRequirements XML elements and Components XML elements within the ApplicationPackage element. </span><span style="font-family: times new roman,times; font-size: 10pt;">RuntimeRequirements specified at the ApplicationPackage level are intended to give an overview of the entire bundle but they may or may not exist depending on the application. Defining the Application RuntimeRequirement section is recommended as it provides faster processing by the product specific Autoloader modules, provides a quicker/easier way for external applications to understand the intended product focus of the App and also provides information about the intended product focus for Apps which have no Components sections (one&#39;s without Autoloader loadable/processable modules).</span>&#0160;</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Defines high level information about the application:</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Attributes:</span></span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">SchemaVersion</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (required): Version number for PackageContents.xml format. Should always be 1.0 until a newer format is released.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">AutodeskProduct</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (required): This field gives an overview of the bundle’s intended Autodesk product. An example would be, you might have a Kitchen application that has been developed on AutoCAD so it is an AutoCAD product, however, you may have data extensions or importers into other products like Revit and Inventor that need to be included in the bundle. Those extensions will of course be loaded by the Revit and Inventor Autoloader, but that does not make your Kitchen application a Revit or Inventor app, it is an AutoCAD app.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">ProductType </span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">(required): This field is used by the AppStore installer team to indicate an “Application” or “Content” installer. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">AppVersion</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (required): Version number for your plug-in application. AutoCAD uses this to determine if an updated version of your application is available and then informs your customer.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">NOTE:</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> In order for the UpgradeCode system to work, you must increment the AppVersion number. It is recommended that the AppVersion is in the format “1.0.0”, or “1.0.0.0” depending on your requirements.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Author</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (optional): Name of the author of the plug-in bundle.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Name</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (required): Name of your plug-in application. If you need localized names you can specify these using NameDeu, NameEsp, NameFra, etc (see full list later in document).</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Description</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (required): Short (one paragraph) description of your plug-in application. Localized descriptions can be specified (see later in document).</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Icon</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (required): Icon to be used to represent your plug-in application in the Apps store. Icon size should be 32x32 pixels and up to 32-bit (truecolor) color depth, we recommend BMP or ICO.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Helpfile</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (required): Location of the file within the package, HTML or PDF. The file can be either the full help or contain information on how to access help. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">SupportedLocales </span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">(optional): this attribute is used by the Autodesk AppPacker tool, it is used to indicate the language types that are supported by the bundle. When this attribute is included, the AppPacker tool reads the delimited string and adds each language locale to the Exchange Store installer MSI.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">AppNameSpace </span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">(optional) : This is an additional app namespace string, it is currently only used by the Autodesk AppManager to indicate Autodesk specific products.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">OnlineDocumentation </span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">(optional) : This is a Uri pointing to any extra documentation that the app utilizes. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&#0160;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">ProductCode</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (required): GUID string used in two ways. First, it is used as an Add/Remove Programs installer ID and secondly it is used by AutoCAD in order to record which applications have been “Bubble Notified” on load. The ProductCode should be updated if the AppVersion changes, this is so upgrade installs will work properly and also so a fresh “Bubble” notification will be displayed for the upgrade when loaded into AutoCAD the first time.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">NOTE:</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> If you deploy your plug-in application bundle through the Autodesk Exchange, the ProductCode will automatically be assigned to your product.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">UpgradeCode</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (optional): <span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&#0160;</span>GUID string which must never be changed. It is a unique identifier used exclusively by the Autodesk Exchange installer. Without this code, upgrade installs will require that the old version be uninstalled, and give a bad user experience. If the code is maintained, the user will install and upgrade with ease.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">NOTE:</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> In order for the UpgradeCode system to work, you must increment the AppVersion number. It is recommended that the AppVersion is in the format “1.0.0”, “1.0.0.0” depending on your requirements.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Element name:</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> CompanyDetails (required)</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Information about your company.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Attributes:</span></span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Name</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (required): Your name or company name.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Phone</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (optional): Your company phone number, localized phone numbers can be specified (see later in document).</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Url</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (required): Your company or product website, localized URLs can be specified (see later in document) – a URL is required for the Autodesk AppStore Digital Signature to be applied to the MSI installer.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Email</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (required): Contact email address, localized email addresses can be specified (see later in document).</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Element name<strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">:</strong> <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">Components</strong> (required)</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">You can specify RuntimeRequirements XML elements and ComponentEntry XML elements within the Components element. RuntimeRequirements specified at the Components level controls whether that Components section is processed by the Autoloader, but they may or may not exist depending on the application.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Contains information about a set of components that make up one part of your application. For example: </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpFirst" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l3 level1 lfo4;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: arial;"><span style="mso-list: ignore;">1.<span style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 7pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span></span><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">A Components section might hold the 32-bit version of your app, another the 64-bit version</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpMiddle" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l3 level1 lfo4;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: arial;"><span style="mso-list: ignore;">2.<span style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 7pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span></span><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">A different Components section might hold your AutoCAD 2011 version and another your 2012 version (you can specify specific RuntimeRequirements element inside of the Components-&gt;ComponentEntry element)</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoListParagraphCxSpLast" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; text-indent: -0.25in; mso-list: l3 level1 lfo4;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-fareast-font-family: arial;"><span style="mso-list: ignore;">3.<span style="line-height: normal;"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman;"><span style="font-size: 7pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span></span><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">A different Components section may contain plugins to other products, for instance, a data import tool for Revit and another for Inventor</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Information on platform, product, and version/series information is defined in the RuntimeRequirements element properties.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">The individual modules specified by ComponentEntry XML elements (see below) within this section are loaded from bottom to top. Therefore, any component on which another component has a dependency must be lower down the list. For example, if an ObjectARX module is dependent on an ObjectDBX module, then the ObjectARX module will appear above the ObjectDBX module in the list.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Different Components elements should not have dependencies on each other. For example, if you have a LSP file that is OS/version independent but depends on an ARX file that is OS/version specific, then you should include the LSP file in each Components element that references the different ARX modules. However, if your LSP file is not dependent on any other files, then it can be broken out into its own (platform/version independent Components element).</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Attributes:</span></span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Description</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (optional): Description of the Components section, this is purely used by the Autodesk AppPacker UI.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Element name:</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> RuntimeRequirements (optional)</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Optionally&#0160;defined as a child elelment of the ApplicationPackage, Components and/or ComponentEntry&#0160;elements. This element&#0160;defines details about the different products types, product versions, platforms, and languages that are supported at the element level that it&#39;s defined. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">You should always include at least an ApplicationPackage RuntimeRequirements, otherwise your bundle will be blindly processed by multiple Autodesk products, potentially incompatible hosts. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">If you do not specify an ApplicationPackage level RuntimeRequirements element, then you must define a RuntimeRequirements element for each Components section you define. Your Components sections RuntimeRequirements element may define multiple Platforms, OSs and series values as long as you define each ComponentEntry with a specific focused&#0160;RuntimeRequirements section to suit.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Attributes:</span></span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">OS</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (optional): Values are ‘Mac’, ‘Win32’, and ‘Win64’. If omitted, it is assumed your application will run on all operating systems – which would only be true for LSP applications and CUIx files, for instance.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Platform</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (optional): <span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&#0160;</span>Indicates the products that the plug-in can be loaded into. Used to specify if the section can be loaded into vanilla AutoCAD or a vertical AutoCAD and can be set to one or more of the following abbreviated strings:</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Civil3D<span style="mso-tab-count: 2;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>- Autodesk Civil 3D</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">AutoCAD <span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>- AutoCAD (AutoCAD* indicates all AutoCAD based products – available from AutoCAD 2012 sp1)</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span lang="PT-BR" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ansi-language: pt-br;"><span style="color: #000000;">Map<span style="mso-tab-count: 2;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>- Map</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span lang="PT-BR" style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ansi-language: pt-br;"><span style="color: #000000;">AIS<span style="mso-tab-count: 2;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>- Inventor Series (AIS)</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">ADT<span style="mso-tab-count: 2;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>- Architectural Desktop</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">ACADM<span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>- AutoCAD Mechanical (ACADM)</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">MEP<span style="mso-tab-count: 2;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>- AutoCAD MEP</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">ACADE<span style="mso-tab-count: 2;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>- AutoCAD Electrical (ACADE)</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">LDT<span style="mso-tab-count: 2;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>- Land Desktop</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">AIP<span style="mso-tab-count: 2;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>- Inventor Professional (AIP)</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">AIPRS<span style="mso-tab-count: 2;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>- Inventor Professional for Routed Systems (AIPRS)</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">AIPSIM <span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>- Inventor Professional for Simulation (AIPSIM)</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">PNID<span style="mso-tab-count: 2;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>- AutoCAD P &amp; ID - 2D</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Plant3D&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; - AutoCAD Plant 3D</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Civil<span style="mso-tab-count: 2;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>- Autodesk Civil</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&#0160;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Other Platform string names (that may or may not be in use currently) are:</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&#0160;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">ecscad </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Simulation Mechanical</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Simulation Moldflow Adviser</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Simulation Moldflow CAD</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Simulation Moldflow Design</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Simulation Moldflow Insight</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Simulation Moldflow Synergy</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Simulation Moldflow Communicator</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Simulation Multiphysics</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Simulation CFD</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Simulation CFD Advanced</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Simulation CFD Motion</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Alias</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Alias*</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Alias Design</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Alias Surface</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Alias Automotive</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Inventor</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Inventor Publisher</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Inventor Factory</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Revit</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Revit Architecture</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Revit Structure</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Revit MEP</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Vault</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&#0160;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Here is an example Platform entry with all of the AutoCAD flavours supported:</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Platform=</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&quot;</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">AutoCAD*|AutoCAD</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&quot;</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&#0160;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Here is an example Platform entry with just the verticals</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="color: #000000;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Platform=</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&quot;</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Civil3D|Map|ADT|ACADM|MEP|ACADE|LDT|PNID|Plant3D|Civil|AIS|AIP|AIPRS|AIPSIM</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&quot;</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&#0160;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">If not included, it is assumed your plugin can be loaded into all AutoCAD and all its vertical applications. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">You may specify multiple products by using the ‘|’ symbol as a separator, for instance Platform=”AutoCAD|Civil3D”. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">AutoCAD 2012 and AutoCAD 2012-based products currently do not support this attribute.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">SeriesMin</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (optional): Defines the minimum release number for ‘this’ set of components. Can be a major release number only (e.g. AutoCAD R18), or specific version (e.g. AutoCAD R18.0). Each Autodesk product has a unique series string. As an example – AutoCAD – R18.0 is the same as the release number in the AutoCAD registry hive. If this and SeriesMax are not specified, then it is assumed these components are compatible with all of the releases, e.g. a LISP file in AutoCAD. If you omit this value than any release lower than SeriesMax is allowed. All none AutoCAD products use their year of the release with a single character prefix depicting the product e.g. R2013 is Revit 2013, V2013 is Vault etc.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">SeriesMax</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (optional): Defines the maximum release number for this set of components. Specified the same as SeriesMin. If you omit this value then any release above <strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">SeriesMin</strong> is allowed. All none AutoCAD products use their year of the release with a single character prefix depicting the product e.g. R2013 is Revit 2013, V2013 is Vault, Ir18 is Inventor 2013&#0160;etc.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">SupportPath</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (optional): Semicolon separated list of support paths used by this set of components (this is normally a relative path to a location within the plug-in application bundle). You may specify a localized version of this attribute if required. This path is added to the product’s Support path – for AutoCAD, the ‘Autoloader’ adds this path to the Files-&gt;Support path Options.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">ToolPalettePath</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (optional): Semicolon separated list of support paths used by this set of components (this is normally a relative path to a location within the plug-in application bundle). You may specify a localized version of this attribute if required. This path is added to the product’s Toolpalette path.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Element name:</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> ComponentEntry (required)</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">You can specify RuntimeRequirements XML elements and Commands XML elements within the ComponentEntry element. RuntimeRequirements specified at the ComponentEntry level controls whether that ComponentEntry section is processed by the Autoloader, but they may or may not exist depending on the application.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">This element is contained within the Components element. It describes specific details about an individual component/module within the Components element. You can specify as many ComponentEntry’s as you like and it may also contain a Commands element if LoadOnCommandInvocation is specified. Component types can be ObjectARX, ObjectDBX, AutoLISP, .NET or partial CUIX.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">IMPORTANT:</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> It is strongly recommended to use LoadOnCommandInvocation if your application defines commands. This is to ensure that AutoCAD startup times are kept as small as possible.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">NOTE:</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (For AutoCAD ARX, DBX and .NET developers only) If the number of ComponentEntry’s in a same Components element is greater than one and at least one ComponentEntry is an ARX, DBX or .NET DLL, then the path defined in the ModuleName attribute of that ComponentEntry will be added to the system PATH. This is so file dependencies are automatically resolved, and any dangers for missing DLL’s are handled as best as possible.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">NOTE: LoadFrom() context issues are automatically handled by the Autodesk product ‘Autoloader’. .NET DLL’s that used to require loading from the host Autodesk product exe folder can now be loaded from folders away from the exe folder. The Autodesk product ‘Autoloader’ implements the AssemblyResolve event which automatically handles this.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">NOTE: For AutoCAD users, partial CUI files that implement WPF custom controls can be declared using the RibbonControls/ RibbonControl and AssemblyMappings/AssemblyMapping elements. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Attributes:</span></span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">AppName</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (Required): Name of this component. For AutoCAD users, this is the same as AcadAppInfo class AppName in ObjectARX API and .NET.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">AppDescription</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (optional): A brief description about this particular component entry. For AutoCAD users, this is the same as AcadAppInfo class AppDescription in ObjectARX API and .NET. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Version</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (recommended): Version number associated with the ComponentEntry. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">ModuleName</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (required): Relative path to component within the bundle. For AutoCAD users, this is the same as AcadAppInfo class ModuleName in ObjectARX API, but it also supports AutoLISP modules also. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">The component type is inferred from the file extension – e.g. for AutoCAD users, ‘arx’ = ObjectARX, ‘dll’ = .NET, ‘lsp’ = AutoLISP, etc. However, you may override this inferred type selection by using the AppType parameter. It is expected that your application will handle multiple languages internally (for example, through the use of resource DLLs). If it is absolutely necessary to ship different versions of a specific component to support different languages, then you can add a suffix to ModuleName attribute to specify multiple languages. (E.g. To support English and French, specify two additional parameters: ModuleNameEnu and ModuleNameFra.) </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">AppType </span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">(optional): The applications type is automatically inferred from the ModuleName attribute’s file extension, however, you may override the inferred application type by using this optional attribute.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">The AutoCAD Autoloader currently processes and recognizes these settings:</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 8pt;">“Bundle“,“ARX“,“Lisp“,“CompiledLisp“,“Dbx“,“.NET“,“Cui“,“CuiX“,“Mnu“ and “Dependency“</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 8pt;">&#0160;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 8pt;">“Dependency” is used where you have a module that should NOT be processed by AutoCAD. An example would be say a licensing DLL, or maybe a resource DLL.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin: 0in 0in 0pt 0.5in; line-height: normal;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 8pt;">&#0160;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">PerDocument</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (optional): Controls the loading of a module when a document is loaded into the editor. For AutoCAD users, if a LSP file should be loaded per document if present, default is True.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">‘<strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><em>LoadReasons</em>’ see below for actual attribute name</strong>&#0160;(optional and multiple): Defines the loading flags for a particular module. For AutoCAD users, see the ObjectARX reference for AcadAppInfo LoadReasons for full details. Set parameter value to &quot;<strong>True&quot;</strong> to enable a load behavior and &quot;<strong>False&quot;</strong> to disable it. With the exception of <em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">LoadOnCommandInvocation</em>, all LoadReasons are enabled by default if not specified. You must explicitly include the LoadReason and set its value to False to disable it. <em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">LoadOnCommandInvocation</em> is a special case – it is disabled by default, and enabling it will disable all other LoadReasons by default (unless they are explicitly enable). </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 1in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong><em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">LoadOnCommandInvocation</span></em></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> – Load only when one of your custom commands is invoked. When using this Load Reason, you must include a ‘Commands’ element. <span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&#0160;</span>Also, if <em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">LoadOnCommandInvocation</em> is enabled, then LoadReasons <em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">LoadOnAutoCADStartup</em><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&#0160; </span>and <em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">LoadOnAppearance</em> are assumed to be disabled unless explicitly enabled. Only applies to ARX and .NET modules.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 1in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong><em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">LoadOnAutoCADStartup</span></em></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> – Load when AutoCAD starts up. If this is specified, then it has precedence over all other LoadReasons. We recommend only using <em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">LoadOnAutoCADStartup</em> when none of the other load reasons are suitable – i.e. you should explicitly disable it (set to False) whenever possible. If the <em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">LoadOnAutoCADStartup</em> parameter is omitted, then it defaults to True; unless <em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">LoadOnCommandInvocation</em> is True, in which case <em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">LoadOnAutoCADStartup</em> defaults to False.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 1in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong><em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">LoadOnProxyDetection</span></em></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> – Load when a proxy for your custom entity is detected. The default is to enable this (i.e. =True) unless it is explicitly set to False (disabled). When enabling <em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">LoadOnProxyDetection</em>, <em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">LoadOnAutoCADStartup</em> should be set to False. Only applies to DBX modules.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 1in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong><em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">LoadOnAppearance</span></em></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> - Load the module as soon as AutoCAD detects the application bundle in its ApplicationPlugins folder, thereby supporting instant load on installation with no need to restart AutoCAD. The property defaults behave the same way as <strong><em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">LoadOnAutoCADStartup</em></strong>, except that the load context is relevant only when an application is installed while AutoCAD is running.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Element name:</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> Commands (required if LoadReason <em style="mso-bidi-font-style: normal;">LoadOnCommandInvocation</em> is specified)</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">You can specify Command XML elements within the Commands element.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">This element specifies command names that should be registered for LoadOnCommandInvocation. It can contain one or more Command elements. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 9pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 8pt;">NOTE:</span></span></strong><span style="line-height: 9pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 8pt;"> Defining LoadOnCommandInvocation=True automatically turns off LoadOnAutoCADStartup and LoadOnAppearance.</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Attributes:</span></span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">GroupName</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (Required): Group name that a command is associated with. This is used in the registry in order to record their existence for inline Command auto complete and for command invocation demand loading. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">You must prefix the GroupName string with your </span><a href="http://usa.autodesk.com/adsk/servlet/index?siteID=123112&amp;id=1075006"><span style="color: #0000ff;">Registered Developer Symbol</span></a><span style="color: #000000;"> text so as to avoid possible name clashing with other products. For AutoCAD users, see the ObjectARX AcadAppInfo documentation for more help.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&#0160;</span></span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Element name:</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> Command (required if Commands element is present)</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Specifies the global and local names for each command.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Attributes:</span></span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Global</span></span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"> (Required): Global name of the command. You must prefix your global commands with your </span><a href="http://usa.autodesk.com/adsk/servlet/index?siteID=123112&amp;id=1075006"><span style="color: #0000ff;">Registered Developer Symbol</span></a><span style="color: #000000;"> text so as to avoid possible name clashing with other products. For AutoCAD users, see the ObjectARX AcadAppInfo documentation for more help.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Local</span></span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"> (Required): Local name of the command. It is highly recommended that you prefix your local commands with your </span><a href="http://usa.autodesk.com/adsk/servlet/index?siteID=123112&amp;id=1075006"><span style="color: #0000ff;">Registered Developer Symbol</span></a><span style="color: #000000;"> text so as to avoid possible name clashing with other products. For AutoCAD users, see the ObjectARX AcadAppInfo documentation for more help. If Multilanguage support is required, the Local attribute can be replaced by LocalEnu, LocalDeu, LocalFra, etc… to specify names for each locale. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">Description</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"> (Required): A single sentence describing what the command does. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">HelpTopic</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">: (Optional) an HTML anchor reference to the ApplicationPackage::HelpFile above. This help topic is invoked when your command is running and F1 is pressed.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="color: #000000;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">StartupCommand</span></strong><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">: (Optional) set to “True” or “False” – if true, then the command will be invoked at startup</span></span></p>
<h2 style="margin: 10pt 0in 0pt;"><a name="_Toc325119027"></a><span style="line-height: 13pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt;"><span style="color: #4f81bd; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-weight: bold;"><span style="text-decoration: none;">Localized attributes</span></span></span></span></h2>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Some attributes mentioned earlier in the document can also be localized by specifying the attribute name and a three letter suffix. The Autoloader checks the running language, if the attribute matches the running language then the localized attribute is used, otherwise the non-localized version of the attribute is used – which should be English. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">So, for example, the ‘Local’ attribute of the ‘Command’ element can be localized as follows:</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">LocalEnu = English</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">LocalDeu = German</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">LocalFra = French</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">LocalEsp = Spanish</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Etc.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Or – the following example shows that German and Spanish are localized, all other language versions use HelpFile (English)</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">HelpFile=”./Contents/Resources/Help.html”</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">HelpFileDeu=”./Contents/Resources/HelpDeu.html”</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">HelpFileEsp=”./Contents/Resources/HelpEsp.html”</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&#0160;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">We recommend you always include a generic (non-localized) parameter to be used in case your plug-in is loaded in a host Autodesk product version you haven’t provided localized information for. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">The locale codes for shipping Autodesk releases are as follows:</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; tab-stops: 1.5in;"><strong style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="FR" style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ansi-language: fr;"><span style="color: #000000;">Locale code<span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>Description</span></span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; tab-stops: 1.5in;"><span lang="FR" style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ansi-language: fr;"><span style="color: #000000;">Chs<span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>Chinese (PRC)</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; tab-stops: 1.5in;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Cht<span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>Chinese (Taiwan)</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; tab-stops: 1.5in;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Csy<span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>Czech</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; tab-stops: 1.5in;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Deu<span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>German</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; tab-stops: 1.5in;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Enu<span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>English</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; tab-stops: 1.5in;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Esp<span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>Spanish</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; tab-stops: 1.5in;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Fra<span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>French</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; tab-stops: 1.5in;"><span lang="DE" style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ansi-language: de;"><span style="color: #000000;">Hun<span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>Hungarian</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; tab-stops: 1.5in;"><span lang="DE" style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ansi-language: de;"><span style="color: #000000;">Ita<span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>Italian</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; tab-stops: 1.5in;"><span lang="DE" style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ansi-language: de;"><span style="color: #000000;">Jpn<span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>Japanese</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; tab-stops: 1.5in;"><span lang="DE" style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-ansi-language: de;"><span style="color: #000000;">Kor<span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>Korean</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; tab-stops: 1.5in;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Plk<span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>Polish</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 0.5in; line-height: 13pt; tab-stops: 1.5in;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Rus<span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span>Russian</span></span></p>
<h2 style="margin: 10pt 0in 0pt;"><a name="_Toc325119028"></a><span style="line-height: 13pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt;"><span style="color: #4f81bd; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-weight: bold;"><span style="text-decoration: none;">Example packages</span></span></span></span></h2>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;">&#0160;</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">The best place to find example packages is on the Autodesk Exchange store, that said, here are some to look at…</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">A LSP files bundle, load one file for each new document and the other just on startup, with a CUIX file. No version, language, or platform version is specified; this is assumed to be compatible with all.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&lt;?</span></span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #a31515;">xml</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #ff0000;">version</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;">=</span></span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">1.0</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #ff0000;">encoding</span></span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">=</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">utf-8</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span></span><span><span style="color: #0000ff; font-size: 6pt;">?&gt;</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&lt;</span></span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #a31515;">ApplicationPackage</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #ff0000;">SchemaVersion</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;">=</span></span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">1.0</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #ff0000;">ProductType</span></span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">=</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">Application</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #ff0000;">Name</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;">=</span></span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">Simple LISP</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #ff0000;">AppVersion</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;">=</span></span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">1.0.0</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span></span></span></p>
