<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 99pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">MypartialCUI.cuix</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 99pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Icon1.ico</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 1in; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #0070c0;">Help</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 6pt 99pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">HelpFile.htm</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">An application consisting of the ObjectARX sample ‘Polysamp’ built for the Mac, Windows 32bit and Windows 64bit – a single bundle defining the runtime for three separate computer platforms. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Notice that the ComponentEntry elements are in reverse dependency order (AutoCAD loads modules from bottom to top). The Windows version would declare the corresponding Components element’s RuntimeRequirements as OS=”Win32” or OS=”Win64” or you can combine them using OS=”Win32|Win64” as seen in the example below.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">The Mac ARX entry has no path specified in the ModuleName, this is because on the Mac an ARX application is already in a .bundle format and therefore the .bundle is the ARX. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Please note the AppDescription for each ComponentEntry, it describes what each represents.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&lt;?</span></span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #a31515;">xml</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #ff0000;">version</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;">=</span></span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">1.0</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #ff0000;">encoding</span></span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">=</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">utf-8</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span></span><span><span style="color: #0000ff; font-size: 6pt;">?&gt;</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&lt;</span></span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #a31515;">ApplicationPackage</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #ff0000;">SchemaVersion</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;">=</span></span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">1.0</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #ff0000;">ProductType</span></span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">=</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">Application</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #ff0000;">ProductCode</span></span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">=</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">{324994BC-1E39-49F5-9B66-3C7549E7F636}</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #ff0000;">UpgradeCode</span></span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">=</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">{224C1293-C62A-4B9C-ABB4-1C09779FB44E}</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #ff0000;">Name</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;">=</span></span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">PolySamp</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span></span></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&#0160; </span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&lt;/</span></span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #a31515;">Components</span></span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff; font-size: 6pt;">&gt;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: 13pt; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217;"><span style="line-height: 7pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&lt;/</span></span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="line-height: 7pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #a31515;">ApplicationPackage</span></span></span><span style="line-height: 7pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff; font-size: 6pt;">&gt;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 7pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 6pt;">&#0160;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">You do not have to enable LoadReason LoadOnProxyDetection for DBX modules, as it is true by default but you do have to disable LoadOnAutoCADStartup or the LoadOnProxyDetection will be overridden with an automatic load. </span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">When LoadOnCommandInvocation is enabled, LoadOnAutoCADStartup is disabled by default; so you do not have to explicitly disable it.</span></span></p>

<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #ff0000;">ModuleNameWin64</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;">=</span></span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">./Contents/Win64/asdkpolyobj64.dbx</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #ff0000;">AppDescription</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;">=</span></span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">Custom Poly DBX Object, even though this loads via proxy detection, it must also be loaded by the ARX UI</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160;&#0160; </span></span></span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #ff0000;">LoadOnProxyDetection</span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;">=</span></span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">True</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span></span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #ff0000;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">LoadOnAutoCADStartup</span></span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;">=</span></span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">False</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #ff0000;">LoadOnAppearance</span></span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">=</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span><span><span style="color: #0000ff;">False</span></span><span style="color: #000000;">&quot;</span></span></span><span style="color: #0000ff;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">/&gt;</span></span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><span style="mso-spacerun: yes;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&#0160; </span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&lt;/</span></span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #a31515;">Components</span></span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff; font-size: 6pt;">&gt;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff; font-size: 6pt;">&#0160;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: normal; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217; mso-layout-grid-align: none;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><span style="font-size: 6pt;">&lt;/</span></span></span><span style="font-size: 6pt;"><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #a31515;">ApplicationPackage</span></span></span><span style="mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt; mso-no-proof: yes;"><span style="color: #0000ff; font-size: 6pt;">&gt;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="background: #d9d9d9; margin: 0in 0in 0pt; line-height: 13pt; mso-background-themecolor: background1; mso-background-themeshade: 217;"><span style="line-height: 7pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000; font-size: 6pt;">&#0160;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">&#0160;</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">No other plug-in modules depend on the LSP modules, so generally speaking they can be kept in their own OS and version independent Components section. If the bundle (ARX) or DBX modules had a dependency on them (or vice versa) then they would have to be included in the Components element on which they depended.</span></span></p>
<h2 style="margin: 10pt 0in 0pt;"><span style="line-height: 13pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt;"><span style="color: #4f81bd; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-weight: bold;"><span style="text-decoration: none;">APPAUTOLOAD AutoCAD Command APPAUTOLOADER Sysvar</span></span></span></span></h2>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Please refer to the AutoCAD documentation for help on the commands that are supported inside of AutoCAD for this feature.</span></span></p>
<h2 style="margin: 10pt 0in 0pt;"><a name="_Toc325119030"></a><span style="line-height: 13pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 13.0pt;"><span style="color: #4f81bd; font-size: 11pt;"><span style="font-weight: bold;"><span style="text-decoration: none;">Limitations</span></span></span></span></h2>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">The new loader mechanism is intended to simplify the most common App deployments. It may not be suitable for some of the more complex installation scenarios. The Autoloader component is not intended to substitute existing App loading architectures, but instead works alongside, so applications not suited to this new mechanism can still be installed using the traditional installation and registration approaches.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">For AutoCAD users, CUIX files must be partial CUIX files only.</span></span></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;">&#0160;</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><strong><span style="line-height: 12pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Update January 24th 2014 by Stephen Preston:</span></span></strong></p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin: 0in 0in 10pt; line-height: 13pt;"><span style="line-height: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><span style="color: #000000;">Alexander Rivilis pointed out that the formatting of the XML examples has become corrupted after Fenton copied the white paper from a Word document to the Typepad editor. (Thanks Alexander).Therefore,&#0160;<a href="http://adndevblog.typepad.com/autocad/Downloads/AutoLoaderWhitePaperv2_3.docx" target="_blank">here is a link to the original Word doc</a> which hopefully has less formatting issues. That said, even the Word document has been formatted for readability as a document and not for simple copying of the XML examples. Also, the formal documentation for the PackageContents.xml format is <a href="http://docs.autodesk.com/ACD/2014/ENU/files/GUID-BC76355D-682B-46ED-B9B7-66C95EEF2BD0.htm" target="_blank">included in the AutoCAD helpfiles</a>, and you can download many free apps from http://apps.exchange.com and open up their accompanying XML files to see lots more examples.</span></span></p>
